# Ada Senior Mastery Quest List

**Total quests:** 1200  
**Concepts:** 120  
**Quest forms per concept:** 10

Each concept repeats through Recall, Explain, Read, Predict, Repair, Write, Test, Refactor, Design, and Senior Review.

## Alire and Ada Foundations

Levels 1–8 · 100 quests · Foundation

### ADA-0001 — Recall: Alire crate lifecycle

- Level: 1
- Type: Recall
- Concept: Alire crate lifecycle
- XP: 60
- Quest: Define Alire crate lifecycle without looking it up. State the Ada rule, the problem it solves, and one misuse to avoid. Focus on creating, building, running, cleaning, and inspecting an Alire crate.

### ADA-0002 — Explain: Alire crate lifecycle

- Level: 1
- Type: Explain
- Concept: Alire crate lifecycle
- XP: 72
- Quest: Explain Alire crate lifecycle to a competent C++ developer who is new to Ada. Compare the closest C++ idea, then explain where the comparison breaks down. Focus on creating, building, running, cleaning, and inspecting an Alire crate.

### ADA-0003 — Read: Alire crate lifecycle

- Level: 1
- Type: Read
- Concept: Alire crate lifecycle
- XP: 84
- Quest: Create or locate a minimal compiling Ada example that demonstrates Alire crate lifecycle. Annotate every line related to the concept and explain how the compiler enforces creating, building, running, cleaning, and inspecting an Alire crate.

### ADA-0004 — Predict: Alire crate lifecycle

- Level: 1
- Type: Predict
- Concept: Alire crate lifecycle
- XP: 96
- Quest: Write a small Ada program involving Alire crate lifecycle. Before building it, predict the compiler result and runtime behavior. Build and run it, then explain every difference between prediction and observation. Focus on creating, building, running, cleaning, and inspecting an Alire crate.

### ADA-0005 — Repair: Alire crate lifecycle

- Level: 1
- Type: Repair
- Concept: Alire crate lifecycle
- XP: 108
- Quest: Start with a minimal working example of Alire crate lifecycle, introduce one realistic defect involving creating, building, running, cleaning, and inspecting an Alire crate, and then repair it. Preserve the diagnostic and explain why the repaired version is correct.

### ADA-0006 — Write: Alire crate lifecycle

- Level: 1
- Type: Write
- Concept: Alire crate lifecycle
- XP: 120
- Quest: From an empty Alire binary crate, implement a focused example of Alire crate lifecycle. Use domain names from avionics, simulation, or game tooling and make creating, building, running, cleaning, and inspecting an Alire crate visible in the design.

### ADA-0007 — Test: Alire crate lifecycle

- Level: 1
- Type: Test
- Concept: Alire crate lifecycle
- XP: 132
- Quest: Add tests for a package that uses Alire crate lifecycle. Include a normal case, a boundary case, and a failure or misuse case related to creating, building, running, cleaning, and inspecting an Alire crate.

### ADA-0008 — Refactor: Alire crate lifecycle

- Level: 1
- Type: Refactor
- Concept: Alire crate lifecycle
- XP: 144
- Quest: Take a working but weak Ada solution involving Alire crate lifecycle and refactor it for stronger typing, clearer package boundaries, and easier testing. Explain how the refactor improves creating, building, running, cleaning, and inspecting an Alire crate.

### ADA-0009 — Design: Alire crate lifecycle

- Level: 1
- Type: Design
- Concept: Alire crate lifecycle
- XP: 156
- Quest: Design a production-quality package or subsystem that depends on Alire crate lifecycle. Specify the public API, hidden representation, contracts, error policy, tests, and dependency direction. Emphasize creating, building, running, cleaning, and inspecting an Alire crate.

### ADA-0010 — Senior Review: Alire crate lifecycle

- Level: 1
- Type: Senior Review
- Concept: Alire crate lifecycle
- XP: 168
- Quest: Perform a senior-level review of an implementation using Alire crate lifecycle. Identify correctness, maintainability, concurrency, performance, portability, and test risks. Recommend a prioritized improvement plan centered on creating, building, running, cleaning, and inspecting an Alire crate.
